 udhar, chennai main samarthan vaapasi par diemke ke daftar main jashn maahaul he

 unka kahana tha ki yadi sarkaar ne diemke kii baat nahin maani tab vah sarkaar se baahar ho jaaegi

 diemke kaa kahana he ki bharat ko is mudde par kade shabdon main srilanka kaa virodh karnaa chahie
 It is alleged that during the ltte's demolition in May 2009, the Sri Lankan army killed many civilians
 diemke kaa kahana he ki is mudde par america kaa prastaav srilanka ke khilaaf bahut majboot nahin he
 He says that there is no talk of an inquiry by the international team in this proposal
 gauratlab he ki teen kendriya mantriyon ne somvaar ko chennai main diemke pramukh em karunanidhi se mulaakaat kii thi or unhen manaane kaa prayaas kiya tha
 These ministers included p Chidambaram, AK Antony and Ghulam Nabi Azad
 kaha ja rahaa he ki is baithak main karunanidhi ne kaha ki bhartiya sansad ko is mudde par ek prastaav paarit karnaa chahie
 It is noteworthy that Samajwadi Party, Bahujan Samaj Party and RJD are also supporting the government from outside
 kul 58 saansad sarkaar ko baahar se samarthan de rahe hai
